			}

function omnitureSearchTerm(sQuery, tipoForm){
      var cachedE=uol_sc.events,cachedLTV=uol_sc.linkTrackVars,cachedLTE=uol_sc.linkTrackEvents||"None",dest='header-buscar';

      if(temp){dest=temp[1];}
      uol_sc.linkType="e";
      uol_sc.prop14=uol_sc.eVar14=sQuery.toLowerCase();
      uol_sc.events="event15,event16";
      uol_sc.prop46=uol_sc.eVar44=dest;
      uol_sc.prop45=uol_sc.eVar42='home2011-'+tipoForm;
        getScrollPage();
      uol_sc.linkTrackVars='prop14,prop19,prop20,prop33,prop34,prop36,prop45,prop46,eVar14,eVar42,eVar44,events';
      uol_sc.linkTrackEvents='event15,event16';

      uol_sc.events=cachedE;
      uol_sc.linkTrackVars=cachedLTV;

}

function clickCounterOmniture(str,drop){
      var cachedE=uol_sc.events,cachedLTV=uol_sc.linkTrackVars,cachedLTE=uol_sc.linkTrackEvents||"None",dest=str;
      var temp=str.match(/.*\-(\w+\-\w+)$/);
      if(temp){dest=temp[1];}
      if(dest=="empregocerto-drop" && drop){
            temp=drop.match(/workingArea\=\w+$/);
            if(temp){dest='http://empregocerto.uol.com.br/info/vagas_por_area.html?'+temp;}
      }
      uol_sc.linkType="e";
      uol_sc.events="event15";
      uol_sc.prop46=uol_sc.eVar44=dest;
      uol_sc.prop45=uol_sc.eVar42='home2011-'+str;
      getScrollPage();
      uol_sc.linkTrackVars="prop19,prop20,prop33,prop34,prop36,prop45,prop46,eVar44,eVar42,events";
      uol_sc.linkTrackEvents='event15';
      uol_sc.tl('clique botao','o',str);
      uol_sc.events=cachedE;
      uol_sc.linkTrackVars=cachedLTV;
      uol_sc.linkTrackEvents=cachedLTE;
}

function getScrollPage(){
uol_sc.prop33=(!uol_sc.prop33?'uol homepage':uol_sc.prop33)
if(uol_sc.prop33){
   uol_sc.prop34=uol_sc.getPercentPageViewed();
   var omtrMaster=(typeof uol_sc.prop34!='undefined'&&uol_sc.prop34!=''&&uol_sc.prop34!='0'?uol_sc.prop34:'2|1'),omtrScrollText=['ate 10%','ate 10%','de 11% a 20%','de 21% a 30%','de 31% a 40%','de 41% a 50%','de 51% a 60%','de 61% a 70%','de 71% a 80%','de 81% a 90%','de 91% a 100%'];
         omtrMaster=omtrMaster.split('|');
  if(omtrMaster){
      var matVisuPage=Math.ceil(omtrMaster[0]/10),matVisuScroll=Math.ceil(omtrMaster[1]/10),matNotScroll=Math.ceil((omtrMaster[0]-omtrMaster[1])/10);
      uol_sc.prop19=omtrScrollText[matVisuPage]+' de visualizacao da pagina';
      uol_sc.prop36=omtrScrollText[matVisuScroll]+' de scroll';
     uol_sc.prop20=omtrScrollText[matNotScroll]+' de visualizacao sem scroll';
  }
}
}

}

function setModulePosition(){
      var i=1, ibox=1, oMod=document.getElementById('modulos'),bGetClass=(typeof document.getElementsByClassName!='undefined');
      if(!oMod) return;
      function getElementsByClassName(classe,noh,tag){
            var aResult=new Array(), tag=tag||'*', noh=noh||document;
            var aEl=noh.getElementsByTagName(tag), iEl=aEl.length;
            var reClass=new RegExp("(^|\\s)"+classe+"(\\s|$)")
            for(var j=0;j<iEl;j++){
                  if(reClass.test(aEl[j].className)){
                        aResult.push(aEl[j]);
                  }
           }
            return aResult;
      }
      function isAncestor(ancestral,elemento){
            if(!elemento) return false;
            var o=elemento.parentNode,body=document.body;
            while(o!=ancestral && o!=body){
                  o=o.parentNode;
            }
            return (o==ancestral?true:false);
      }
      function setClickOmtr(aLinks,clkVal){
            if(!aLinks) return false;
            var iLinks=aLinks.length;
            for(var k=0;k<iLinks;k++){
                  aLinks[k].clickomtr=clkVal;
            }
      }
      function setSubModuloPosition(oModV, str){
            var vMods = bGetClass? oModV.getElementsByClassName('moduloVertical'):getElementsByClassName('moduloVertical',oModV,'div'), j=1, iMods=vMods.length;
            for(var k=0;k<iMods;k++){
                  if(!isAncestor(vMods[k],document.getElementById('banner-300x250-5-Area'))){
                        setClickOmtr(vMods[k].getElementsByTagName('a'),(str+'-v'+j));
                        j++;
                  }
            }
      }
      var aModChildren=oMod.childNodes,iModChildren=aModChildren.length,aModChildrenDivs=new Array();
      for(var j=0;j<iModChildren;j++){
          if(aModChildren[j].nodeName.toLowerCase()=='div'){
              aModChildrenDivs.push(aModChildren[j])
         }
      }
      var iModChildrenDivs=aModChildrenDivs.length,oModVe=document.getElementById('moduloVerticalEsquerda'),oModVd=document.getElementById('moduloVerticalDireita');
      for(var j=0;j<iModChildrenDivs;j++){
            if(aModChildrenDivs
ab3
[j].className.match(/(^|\s)moduloHorizontal|moduloAoVivo(\s|$)/)){
                  var aLinks=aModChildrenDivs[j].getElementsByTagName('a');
                  setClickOmtr(aModChildrenDivs[j].getElementsByTagName('a'),('m'+i))
                  i++;
            } else if(isAncestor(aModChildrenDivs[j],oModVe) && isAncestor(aModChildrenDivs[j],oModVd)){
                  setSubModuloPosition(oModVe,'m'+i+'e');
                  setSubModuloPosition(oModVd,'m'+i+'d');
          i++;
            }
      }
      
      var oBox=document.getElementById('corpoDireita');
      if(oBox){
            var oBoxes = bGetClass? oBox.getElementsByClassName('box'):getElementsByClassName('box',oBox,'div'), iBox=oBoxes.length;
            for(var j=0;j<iBox;j++){
                  setClickOmtr(oBoxes[j].getElementsByTagName('a'),('b'+ibox));
                  ibox++;
            }
      }
}
